<tr>
<th>Misc. Notes
</th>
<td>Some of them are out of order. The key sequence should be chromatic with each major key followed by its subdominant minor (C, f, Db, f#, D, g, etc.) Thus the correct order (going by the numbers given in this edition) should be: 1, 2, 3, 4, 5, 6, 7, 8, 10, 11, 9, 14, 12, 13, 16, 17, 15, 18, 20, 19, 21, 22, 23, 24, 25.
</td></tr>

<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="Misc._Comments">Misc. Comments</span></h2>
<p>WA Eddie, in Charles Valentin Alkan: His Life And His Music, seems to date the composition of the Preludes closer to 1844?
